 luthra ne kaha ki jaanch abhi praarambhik charan main he or hiraasat main lekar kanda se poochtacha karnaa jaruri he
 Significantly, the court of Sessions Judge dismissed Kanda's anticipatory bail plea on August 6, saying that the charges against him were worrying and serious and there was no merit in his petition on the basis of which the bail was granted
 kanda ke khilaaf geetika ko aatmahatya ke liye uksaane or dhamkaane kaa maamla darj he
 The comments kanda ne chote vyavsaayee ke rup main apane kariyar kii shuruyaat kii thi or baad main property dealer banakar karodon main khilne lage
 In the year 2007, he started MDLR Airlines
 oktober 2009 ke chunaav main vah sirsa se nirdaleey ummidavaar ke rup main haryana vidhansabha ke liye nirvaachit hue the
 He had secured the ministerial position by supporting the Congress government led by Bhupendra Singh Hooda
 dilli police kii ore se pesh atirikt mahadhivaktaa siddharth luthra ne poochtacha ke liye kanda kii hiraasat kii maang kii, taaki kanda or unki company kii varisht adhikari aruna chaddha ke bich sajeesh kaa pataa chal sake
 Senior advocate KTS Tulsi, representing Kanda, told the Delhi High Court that the suicide note cannot be considered as 'absolute truth'
 kanda agrim jamaanat chaahate hai
 Tulsi said, "suicide notes are written in anger and any allegations can be made in anger
 " unhone kaha ki geetika ke likhe suicide noton ko purna nahin mana ja saktaa
 It is to be known that the girl, who was an air hostess, hanged her in the fan of her house on the night of August 4-5
 usne do suicide note likhe the, jinamein usne aatmahatya ke liye kanda or kanda kii company kii varisht adhikari aruna chaddha ko jimmedaar tehraaya tha
 Aruna is arrested while Kanda goes underground
 tulsi ne kanda kii taraf se kaha, "ho saktaa he, vah mujhe acchhee lagati ho yaa main use acha lagata houn lekin iskaa yah arth nahin ki maine use aatmahatya ke liye uksaaya
 "he said that some other evidence is necessary to hold Kanda responsible for Geetika's suicide
 tulsi ne kaha, "nichali adaalat ne agrim jamaanat kharij karte hue jo kaaran bataae hai, ve hai adhikaar kaa durupyog, geetika ke prati adhik meharbaani dikhaanaa or uskaa shoshan karnaa, lekin ye aparaadh aatmahatya ke liye uksaane ke daayre main nahin aate
 "he said Geetika was a self-respecting girl and could not think of committing suicide
 tulsi ne kanda kii ore se daleel di, "yahaan tak ki uski maa or uskaa bhai bhi nahin jaanata tha ki vah aatmahatya kar sakati he to phir mujhe kaise pataa chal saktaa he
 " vahiin, siddharth luthra ne kanda kii agrim jamaanat yachika kaa virodh kiya
 He said, "he is not cooperating in the investigation and has removed all electronic items including laptops and computers from his office
" aise main unhen agrim jamaanat nahin di jaani chahie
 " police ke vakil ne adaalat se kaha, "hamen jaanch main samasya aa rahi he
 When we reached Kanda's office, all the computers had been removed from there
 " unhone adaalat se apil kii ki kanda kii agrim jamaanat yachika khaarij kar di jaae, kyonki jaanch main sahyog ke liye notice di jane ke baavjood vah faraar ho gaye
 Luthra said that the investigation is still in the initial stage and it is necessary to interrogate Kanda from custody
 gauratlab he ki satr nyaayadhish kii adaalat ne kanda kii agrim jamaanat yachika chah agast ko yah kehete hue khaarij kar di thi ki unke khilaaf aarope chintajanak or sangeen hai or unki yachika main aisi koi khubi nahin he, jis aadhaar par jamaanat de di jaae
 Kanda has a case of abetment to suicide and bullying Geetika

 rajya sarkaar ke ek pravaktaa ne kaha ki mukhyamantri ne krishi niryaat rajya mantri swati singh ke ek bear baar kaa udghaatan kiye jane ke sambandh main media main prasaarit khabaron kaa sangyaan liya he
 The UP government spokesman said that the Chief Minister has asked Swati Singh to clarify the situation after getting information about the entire case
 yogi ne kaarykram main shaamil hue adhikariyon se spashtikaran praapt karne ke nirdesh bhi diye hai
 The move has been taken by the government after pictures of Swati Singh's one-time bar inauguration went viral on social media
 swati singh ne di safivahin, maamle main swati singh ne safai di he
 He said, 'I have inaugurated the restaurant
 maamle ko bevajaah tool diya ja rahaa he
 The restaurant belongs to my friend
 mujhe isaki zyada jaankaree nahin thi
 The restaurant owner had taken the license for just three days
 unhen yahaan bear baar nahin chalaanaa he or na hi iske license kii arji di he
 'what's the matter? Photos of Swati Singh, Minister of State in the UP government, are being voiced on social media in which she is seen inaugurating a beer bar
 vipakshi dalon kii ore se photo viral hone ke baad sarkaar kii kaaryastylee par sawaal uthaae gaye hai
 Swati Singh, BJP MLA from Sarojini Nagar, inaugurated a friend's beer bar in the capital on May 20
 kaarykram main shaamil hue prashasnic adhikariyon se bhi safai maangi gai he
 There has been controversy in the past, even before she became a minister, she was in the news
 swati ke pati or bijepi netaa dayashankar singh ne bispi supremeo mayawati par abhadra bayaan diya tha, jiske baad party ne unhen chah saal ke liye nilambit kar diya tha
 Swati Singh openly defended her husband in the media
 haalanki bijepi ne baad main dayashankar kaa nilamban radd kar unhen waapas party main le liya tha

 party ke bheetar tut-foot or antarkalah se uske alpsankhyak vot bank ko yahi sanket jayega ki vah itani kamjor he ki bijepi kii chunauti kaa muqabla nahin kar sakati
 Due to such strategic multiplication, minority vote bank can clearly go towards BSP
 yahi nahin, bijepi apane mandal avatar main sargarmi ke saath obisi or embisi voton kii talash main he
 It can dent OBC votes including sp's Yadavs
 aakhirkaar padosi bihar main 2014 main bhagava party ne yadavon par argedy netaa lalu prasad ke ekadhikaar main send laga hi di thi
 In the Samajwadi Party, if there is any leader who can take all the factions together and also stand a grand alliance as well, then they are just soft
 tamaam gahamagahami or naatak or antarkalah ke baavjood, chaahe vah shivpal hon yaa amar singh, akhilesh hon yaa ramgopal, sabhi netaji kii aguai kii kasame khate hai
 In the evening of his life, he is the only gum or mustard who can keep the party together
 unhone bahut sooyeeboojh se ek khel khelaa—ve jaanate the ki party tut kii taraf bad rahi he, khaskar tikat bantwaare ko lekar, jab shivpal ke walk out kii puri sambhaavna hoti, unhen party main roke rakhane ke liye mulaayam had se aage chale gaye, duusari taraf unhone akhilesh ke hiton kii bhi puri hifaazat kii
 Not only this, if Akhilesh has youth and charisma in his favor, Shivpal has the experience of 25 years to build the party
 or amar singh or ramgopal bhale hi aankh se aankh na milaate hon, magar donon hi nepathy kii raajnneeti ke behtareen manje hue khilaadi hai or donon ke hi bagaiyr party kaa kaam nahin chal saktaa
 Perhaps the time has come for the Samajwadi Party to understand that whatever their differences may be, together they can still be a winning team
 supreme court ne kaha ki vah samay kii kami kii vajah se sirf ‘teen talaak’ par sunwaayee karegaa lekin kendra ke jor ke maddenjar bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke muddon ko bhavishya main sunwaayee ke liye khulaa rakh rahaa he, supreme court main centre kii ore se atorni general ne kaha ki centre sarkaar teen talaak par kanoon banane ko taiyaar he
 He said that there is no vacuum on this issue
 kender ne kaha ki supreme court teen talaak, bahuvivaah or halaala ko radd kare
 Explain that the Supreme Court has said what will happen if the three forms of triple talaq i
e
, talaq-e-biddat, talaq-e-lasana and abolition of divorce are canceled
 On this, the AG said that the government is ready to bring the law
 isse pehle AG ne kaha - In the case of divorce, women's rights in Muslim society are lower than men
 desh main anya samudaayon kii mahilaon kii tulana main muslim mahilaon ko samaan adhikaar nahin
 Women of Muslim community in India have less rights than women in Islamic countries abroad, where a law was enacted as a reform on marriage and divorce
 AG ne supreme court main kaha - Marriage, divorce have nothing to do with religion or religious practice
 kisi ke jivan ko kaise niyantrit kiya ja saktaa he
 The court is not meant to interpret the Holy Quran, the Guru Granth Sahib or the Gita
 centre ne supreme court se kaha - If the Supreme Court quits triple talaq, nikah halala and bahuivah, then the Center is ready to bring a law on it
 is mudde par koi vaikum nahin rahegaa The AG gave this argument at a time when the court asked that if the court quashed it, what option would Muslim husbands have? AG ne supreme court main kaha - The triple talaq is contrary to the constitution
 ye mahilaon ke samanta, langik samanta or maanavadhikaar ke khilaaf he
 Any personal person or practice, it has to go through the criteria of the constitution
 personal laa kii bhi samanta ke adhikaar, langik samanta ke adhikaar se tulana honi chahie
 Any woman should have the same rights as women of other communities
 AG ne court main kaha - This is a sensitive issue related to minorities, so the old government did not bring a law on it - puraane granthon se liye gaye personal laa bhi samvidhan ke mutabik hone chahine Half of the Muslim population is feeling helpless due to triple talaq
 - desh main ek samudaay ke nagarikon ko puure moulik adhikaar nahin mil rahe hai
 Kapil Sibal said in the Supreme Court on behalf of AIMPLB
 
 
 - har samudaay main mahilaon ke saath bhedbhaav hota he According to Hindu law, it is up to the father to give the daughter a share in the property or not
 - lekin muslim lau main pita ko chauthai hissaa beti ko dena hi hota he - Isn't this discrimination - aap kya chaahate hai ki hinduon main beti ko bina koi pai mili wo saalon tak talaak ke liye ladati rahen a five-member constitution bench headed by CJI JS Khehar said, "in the limited time we have, it is not possible to address all three issues
" ham unhen bhavishya ke liye lambit rakhenge
 The court said this when Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi, appearing on behalf of the Central Government, said that the order of the two-member bench which has been presented before the Constitution Bench includes 'triple talaq' with polygamy and 'nikah halala'
 Issues are also included
 kendra kii yah baat court kii is tippanee ke maddenjar ahm he ki vah sirf ‘teen talaak’ kaa mudda nibataayega or vah bhi tab jab yah islam ke liye buniyadi mudda hoga
 The bench consists of Justice Kurian Joseph, Justice RF Nariman, Justice UU Lalit and Justice Abdul Nazir
 rohtagi ne samvidhan peeth se yah saaf karne ke liye kaha ki bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke mudde ab bhi khule hai or koi or peeth bhavishya main ise nibataayegi
 "these will be dealt with in future," the court clarified
 ’’ ucchtam nyaayalay muslim samaaj main vyaapt teen talaak ko chunauti dene vaali yachikaaon par sunwaayee kar rahi he
 The Center has started presenting its arguments today
 pichhali sunwaayee main supreme court ne kai bade sawaal uthaae the
 The court said that triple talaq is the worst and undesirable way to end marriage in Islam
 haalanki tripal talaak ko islam ke vibhinn skool of thats main ise vaid mana gaya he
 Is triple divorce a part of tradition or Sharia? kya jo dharm ke mutabik hi ghinauna he wo kanoon ke tahat vaid tehraaya ja saktaa he? jo ishwar kii najar main paap he kya use shariat main liya ja saktaa he? bahut saare log desh main maut kaa sajaa ko sin yani paap maanate hai lekin kanuunan ye vaid he
 If triple divorce is specific in India, then other countries have enacted laws and abolished triple divorce? (first day hearing: Supreme Court on triple talaq case - if it is a matter of religion then the court will not interfere in it) Comments vahiin nijee taur par court kii madad kar rahe purv kanoon mantri or congressi netaa salmaan khurshid ne kaha tha ki meri nijee raay main tripal talaak paap he, lekin AIMPLB kaa stand he ki tripal talaak ghinauna he lekin tab bhi vaid he
 At the same time, the All India Muslim Women Personal Law Board has also declared the triple talaq illegal
 bataa den ki supreme court ne kaha he ki teen talaak kii teenon farm yani talaak e biddat, talaak e hasana or talaak ke ahasan ko radd kar diya jaae ko kya hoga ? is par AG ne kaha sarkaar kanoon laane ko taiyaar he
 Earlier the AG said - talaak ke maamle main muslim samaaj main mahilaon ke adhikaar purushon kii tulana main kam
 Muslim women do not have equal rights as compared to women from other communities in the country
 videshon main um islamic deshon kii mahilaon ke mukaable bharat main muslim samudaay kii mahilaon ke adhikaar kam jahaan shaadi or talaak ko lekar rifarm ke taur par kanoon banaaya gaya
 The AG said in the Supreme Court - shaadi, talaak kaa dharm yaa dharmik pratha se koi lenaa dena nahin
 How can one's life be controlled
 court pavitra quran, guru granth sahib yaa gita kii vyakhya karne ke liye nahin he
 The Center told the Supreme Court - agar supreme court teen talaak, nikaah halaala or bahoovivaah ko radd kar detaa he to centre is par kanoon laane ko taiyaar
 There will be no vacuum on this issue AG ne ye daleel us vakt di jab court ne poocha ki agar court ise radd kar detaa he to muslim patiyon ke paas kya vikalp hoga ? The AG said in the Supreme Court - teen talaak samvidhan ke vipareet he
 It is against women's equality, gender equality and human rights
 koi bhi personal laa ho yaa pratha, use samvidhan kii kasuti se guzarana hoga
 Personal law should also be compared to right to equality, right to gender equality
 kisi bhi mahila ko duusare samudaay kii mahilaon ke samaan haq hona chahie
 AG said in court - ye minerti se juda samvedansheel mudda he isliye puraani sarkaar is par kanoon nahin laai - Personal laws taken from old texts should also be according to the constitution - teen talaak kii vajah se muslimon main aadhi aabaadi asahaay mahasoos kar rahi he - The citizens of a community in the country are not getting full fundamental rights
 AIMPLB kii ore se kapil sibbal ne supreme court main kaha
 
 
 - Women are discriminated against in every community - hindu lau ke mutabik pita par hota he ki wo beti ko jaaydaad main hissaa de yaa nahin - But in Muslim law, father has to give quarter to daughter
 - kya ye bhedbhaav nahin he - What do you want the daughter of Hindus to fight for divorce for years without getting any pie? sijeai jees khehar kii adhyakshata vaali paanch sadasyeey samvidhan peeth ne kaha, ‘‘hamaare paas jo simit samay he usamen teenon muddon ko nibataana sambhav nahin he
 We will keep them pending for the future
 ’’ adaalat ne yah baat tab kahi jab kendra sarkaar kii ore se pesh atarni general mukul rohtagi ne kaha ki do sadasyeey peeth ke jis aadesh ko samvidhan peeth ke samaksh pesh kiya gaya he usamen ‘teen talaak’ ke saath bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke mudde bhi shaamil hai
 The Centre's view is significant in view of the court's comment that it will only deal with the issue of 'triple talaq' and that too when it is a fundamental issue for Islam
 peeth main nyaayamurti courian joseph, nyaayamurti aaref nariman, nyaayamurti yuyuu lalit or nyaayamurti abdul nazeer shaamil hai
 Rohatgi asked the Constitution Bench to make it clear that issues of polygamy and 'nikah halala' are still open and another bench will deal with it in future
 adaalat ne spasht kiya, ‘‘inhen bhavishya main nibataya jayega
 The Supreme Court is hearing petitions challenging the three divorces prevalent in Muslim society
 kendra ne aaj apni daleelein pesh kerani shuru kii he
 In the previous hearing, the Supreme Court raised many big questions
 court ne kaha tha ki teen talaak islam main shaadi khatm karne kaa sabase bura or avaanchhneeya tarika he
 Although triple divorce has been recognized as valid in various schools of Islam
 tripal talaak kya parampara he yaa shariat kaa hissaa he? Can one who is disgusted according to religion be valid under the law? What is a sin in the eyes of God, can it be taken in the Shari'a? Many people consider the death penalty to be a sin in the country, but it is valid by law
 agar bharat main tripal talaak vishisht he to duusare deshon ne kanoon banaakar tripal talaak ko khatm kar diya? (pehle din kii sunwaayee : teen talaak maamle par supreme court - agar yah dharm kaa maamla he to court isamen dakhal nahin degi)tippaniyan At the same time, former Law Minister and Congress leader Salman Khurshid, who is personally assisting the court, said that in my personal opinion triple divorce is a sin, but AIMPLB stands that triple divorce is abusive but still valid
 vahiin, ol india muslim mahila personal laa board ne bhi teen talaak ko gaiyrkanoonee qaraar diya he

 Is triple divorce a part of tradition or Sharia? kya jo dharm ke mutabik hi ghinauna he wo kanoon ke tahat vaid tehraaya ja saktaa he? jo ishwar kii najar main paap he kya use shariat main liya ja saktaa he? bahut saare log desh main maut kaa sajaa ko sin yani paap maanate hai lekin kanuunan ye vaid he
 If triple divorce is specific in India, then other countries have enacted laws and abolished triple divorce? (first day hearing: Supreme Court on triple talaq case - if it is a matter of religion then the court will not interfere in it) Comments vahiin nijee taur par court kii madad kar rahe purv kanoon mantri or congressi netaa salmaan khurshid ne kaha tha ki meri nijee raay main tripal talaak paap he, lekin AIMPLB kaa stand he ki tripal talaak ghinauna he lekin tab bhi vaid he
 At the same time, the All India Muslim Women Personal Law Board has also declared the triple talaq illegal
 AG ne supreme court main kaha - The triple talaq is contrary to the constitution
 ye mahilaon ke samanta, langik samanta or maanavadhikaar ke khilaaf he
 Any personal person or practice, it has to go through the criteria of the constitution
 personal laa kii bhi samanta ke adhikaar, langik samanta ke adhikaar se tulana honi chahie
 Any woman should have the same rights as women of other communities
 AG ne court main kaha - This is a sensitive issue related to minorities, so the old government did not bring a law on it - puraane granthon se liye gaye personal laa bhi samvidhan ke mutabik hone chahine Half of the Muslim population is feeling helpless due to triple talaq
 - desh main ek samudaay ke nagarikon ko puure moulik adhikaar nahin mil rahe hai
 Kapil Sibal said in the Supreme Court on behalf of AIMPLB
 
 
 - har samudaay main mahilaon ke saath bhedbhaav hota he According to Hindu law, it is up to the father to give the daughter a share in the property or not
 - lekin muslim lau main pita ko chauthai hissaa beti ko dena hi hota he - Isn't this discrimination - aap kya chaahate hai ki hinduon main beti ko bina koi pai mili wo saalon tak talaak ke liye ladati rahen a five-member constitution bench headed by CJI JS Khehar said, "in the limited time we have, it is not possible to address all three issues
" ham unhen bhavishya ke liye lambit rakhenge
 The court said this when Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi, appearing on behalf of the Central Government, said that the order of the two-member bench which has been presented before the Constitution Bench includes 'triple talaq' with polygamy and 'nikah halala'
 Issues are also included
 kendra kii yah baat court kii is tippanee ke maddenjar ahm he ki vah sirf ‘teen talaak’ kaa mudda nibataayega or vah bhi tab jab yah islam ke liye buniyadi mudda hoga
 The bench consists of Justice Kurian Joseph, Justice RF Nariman, Justice UU Lalit and Justice Abdul Nazir
 rohtagi ne samvidhan peeth se yah saaf karne ke liye kaha ki bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke mudde ab bhi khule hai or koi or peeth bhavishya main ise nibataayegi
 "these will be dealt with in future," the court clarified
 ’’ ucchtam nyaayalay muslim samaaj main vyaapt teen talaak ko chunauti dene vaali yachikaaon par sunwaayee kar rahi he
 The Center has started presenting its arguments today
 pichhali sunwaayee main supreme court ne kai bade sawaal uthaae the

 At the same time, the All India Muslim Women Personal Law Board has also declared the triple talaq illegal
 AIMPLB kii ore se kapil sibbal ne supreme court main kaha
 
 
 - Women are discriminated against in every community - hindu lau ke mutabik pita par hota he ki wo beti ko jaaydaad main hissaa de yaa nahin - But in Muslim law, father has to give quarter to daughter
 - kya ye bhedbhaav nahin he - What do you want the daughter of Hindus to fight for divorce for years without getting any pie? sijeai jees khehar kii adhyakshata vaali paanch sadasyeey samvidhan peeth ne kaha, ‘‘hamaare paas jo simit samay he usamen teenon muddon ko nibataana sambhav nahin he
 We will keep them pending for the future
 ’’ adaalat ne yah baat tab kahi jab kendra sarkaar kii ore se pesh atarni general mukul rohtagi ne kaha ki do sadasyeey peeth ke jis aadesh ko samvidhan peeth ke samaksh pesh kiya gaya he usamen ‘teen talaak’ ke saath bahuvivaah or ‘nikaah halaala’ ke mudde bhi shaamil hai
 The Centre's view is significant in view of the court's comment that it will only deal with the issue of 'triple talaq' and that too when it is a fundamental issue for Islam
 peeth main nyaayamurti courian joseph, nyaayamurti aaref nariman, nyaayamurti yuyuu lalit or nyaayamurti abdul nazeer shaamil hai
 Rohatgi asked the Constitution Bench to make it clear that issues of polygamy and 'nikah halala' are still open and another bench will deal with it in future
 adaalat ne spasht kiya, ‘‘inhen bhavishya main nibataya jayega
 The Supreme Court is hearing petitions challenging the three divorces prevalent in Muslim society
 kendra ne aaj apni daleelein pesh kerani shuru kii he
 In the previous hearing, the Supreme Court raised many big questions
 court ne kaha tha ki teen talaak islam main shaadi khatm karne kaa sabase bura or avaanchhneeya tarika he
 Although triple divorce has been recognized as valid in various schools of Islam
 tripal talaak kya parampara he yaa shariat kaa hissaa he? Can one who is disgusted according to religion be valid under the law? What is a sin in the eyes of God, can it be taken in the Shari'a? Many people consider the death penalty to be a sin in the country, but it is valid by law
 agar bharat main tripal talaak vishisht he to duusare deshon ne kanoon banaakar tripal talaak ko khatm kar diya? (pehle din kii sunwaayee : teen talaak maamle par supreme court - agar yah dharm kaa maamla he to court isamen dakhal nahin degi)tippaniyan At the same time, former Law Minister and Congress leader Salman Khurshid, who is personally assisting the court, said that in my personal opinion triple divorce is a sin, but AIMPLB stands that triple divorce is abusive but still valid
 vahiin, ol india muslim mahila personal laa board ne bhi teen talaak ko gaiyrkanoonee qaraar diya he
 a five-member constitution bench headed by CJI JS Khehar said, "in the limited time we have, it is not possible to address all three issues
" ham unhen bhavishya ke liye lambit rakhenge
 The court said this when Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi, appearing on behalf of the Central Government, said that the order of the two-member bench which has been presented before the Constitution Bench includes 'triple talaq' with polygamy and 'nikah halala'
 Issues are also included
 kendra kii yah baat court kii is tippanee ke maddenjar ahm he ki vah sirf ‘teen talaak’ kaa mudda nibataayega or vah bhi tab jab yah islam ke liye buniyadi mudda hoga
 The bench consists of Justice Kurian Joseph, Justice RF Nariman, Justice UU Lalit and Justice Abdul Nazir

 uttar pradesh ke mukhyamantri yogi adityanath ke kade nirdesh ke baavjood abhi tak lagbhag 120 iees adhikariyon ne apni sampatti kaa byoraa nahin diya he
 The Yogi government had asked the officers to give details of their movable and immovable property
 adhikariyon ko pehle 15 din kaa mauka diya gaya tha
 After this, the period was extended again, but even after the expiry of the period on Tuesday, 120 IAS officers did not give details of their movable property and 30 of their immovable property
 iske baad ab mukhya sachiv ne teen may tak is silsile main sabhi vibhaagon ke pramukh sachivon se byoraa uplabdh karaane ko kaha he

 unhone kaha ki achal sampatti kaa byoraa to adhikari har saal jamaa karte hai

 iske baad bhi byoraa nahin mila

 2) minimum 30 gram sona jamaa karnaa hogarishbhi dwaara jari disha nirdeshon ke mutabik is yojana main kam se kam 30 gram 995 shuddhta vaala sona bank main rakhana hoga jabaki adhiktam kii koi seemaa nahin he
 This will include gold bars, coins, jewelry etc
 dhyaan rahen ki isamen metal shaamil nahin hoga
 3) Banks will decide on their own interest rate
 All commercial banks are allowed to start this scheme
 iske saath hiarbiai ne ye bhi anumati de di heki sabhi bank jamaa sone par khud byaaj daren tay kar sakate hai
 4) Gold check before depositing: In this scheme, gold can be deposited in three ways
 short turm (1 se 3 saal), medium turm (5 se 7 saal) or long turm (12 se 15 saal)
 Also, before depositing the gold, its purity will be checked
 iske baad hi jamaa karne sambandhi kaam aage badhaayaa ja sakegaa
 5) Option to take money or gold At the end of the maturity period, you will have the option to either take money or withdraw your gold
 acchhee baat yah he ki aapako bhugtan us samay sone kii keemat ke anusaar hi kiya jayega
 Only when you go to deposit gold will you be asked which option you are going to choose
 dhyaan rahen kiap ise baad main badal nahin sakate

 ) The Supreme Court has expressed concern over unnatural deaths including suicide during detention in the country's jails
 supreme court ne sabhi hoicourt ke chif justise se kaha he ki jail main khudakushi samet sabhi aprakritik mauton ke maamalon main kaidi ke parivaar ko uchit muaavja dene ke liye swat: sangyaan lekar janhit yachika darj karen
 According to the data given by the National Crime Records Bureau (NCRB), orders should be made to trace all the cases of unnatural deaths in jails between 2012 and 2015 and to provide appropriate compensation to their families
 supreme court ne apane ek mahatvapurn faisle main jail sudhaar ke liye ye dishanirdesh jari kiye hai
 According to them
 
 
 - sarkaar ko 'open jail' kii vyavastha par vichaar karne kii jarurat he
 Health services within the prison need to be repaired to prevent unnatural deaths of prisoners in jails
 - jail kaa naam badalakar 'sudhaar grih' karne se keval baat nahin banegi
 Adequate measures need to be taken for this
 - kaidiyon ke sudhaar ke liye ek board banaaya janaa chahie jisamen samaaj ke prabud logon ko shaamil kiya jaay jo model jail manual kaa lagu karaaye or kaidiyon ke sudhaar main sahyog karen
 - The Central Government should issue advisory in this regard to all the states and tell that investigation of such deaths is also necessary
 rajya sarkaron dwaara is kaam ko 30 november tak puraa kiya janaa chahie
 - The meeting of prisoners with family members should be encouraged
 sarkaar ko kaidiyon se mulaakaat ke samay ko badhaane or mulaakaat ke avasar badhaane par vichaar karnaa chahie
 - In addition, phone and video conferencing possibilities should be considered for interaction between prisoners and their families
 - na keval parijanon se baatcheet ke liye balki kaidiyon kii unke vakil se baat ke liye bhi is par vichaar hona chahie
 The Supreme Court said that the government should prepare a strategy to prevent incidents of self-murder by inmates in jails, so that such incidents can be stopped
 - supreme court ne kaha ki grih mantralay NCRB ko aadesh jari kare ki vah apane data main prakritik or aprakritik maut ke antar ko spasht kare
 - The government needs to consider the system of 'open prison'
 - jelon main kaidiyon ke aprakritik maut ko rokane ke liye jail ke bheetar swasthya sevaaon ko durust karne kii jarurat he
 - Changing the name of the jail to 'correctional Home' will not be the only thing
 iske liye paryaapt upaay karne kii jarurat he
 a board should be formed for the improvement of prisoners, involving enlightened people of the society who implement the model prison manual and cooperate in the improvement of prisoners
 - centre sarkaar sabhi rajyon ko is sambandh main adwyjuri jari kare or bataae ki aisi mauton kii jaanch bhi jaruri he
 This work should be completed by November 30 by the state governments
 - parijanon se kaidiyon se mulaakaat ko badhaava dena chahie
 The government should consider extending the time of meeting with prisoners and increasing the opportunity of meeting
 - iske alaava kaidiyon ore unke parijanon ke bich baatcheet ke liye phone or video confrencing kii sambhaavnaaon par vichaar kiya janaa chahie
 - This should be considered not only for the interaction with the family but also for the prisoners to talk to their lawyer

 1
 sabase pehle jo topic aapane taiyaar kiye hai unhencchhi tarah se doharaa len
 If you are thinking about reading a new topic, do not do it because at the end of the exam, the introduction of a new topic confuses you
 2
 Create a revision time-table so that you know exactly what is left to study and what is left
 3
 Repeat all the formulas again, you will not get the problem by doing this
 4
 Do not forget the group study at the end of the exam

 5
 puraane paper or queshchanbankko solve kar khud ko test karen
